  代码:
    import pandas as pd
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    import numpy as np
    import seaborn as sns
    import os
    
    # 读取数据
    df = pd.read_excel(os.environ['DATASET_PATH'])
    
    print("=" * 60)
    print("📊 数据基本特征分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 1. 数据概览
    print(f"📈 数据集大小: {df.shape[0]} 行 × {df.shape[1]} 列")
    print(f"✅ 数据完整性: 100% (无缺失值)")
    print(f"💾 内存占用: {df.memory_usage(deep=True).sum() / 1024 / 1024:.2f} MB")
    
    # 2. 渠道结构分析
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📢 投放渠道结构")
    print("=" * 60)
    channel_stats = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '曝光数': ['count', 'sum', 'mean'],
        '访问数': ['sum', 'mean'],
        '留资人数': ['sum', 'mean'],
        '转化金额': ['sum', 'mean'],
        '投放成本': ['sum', 'mean']
    }).round(2)
    
    channel_stats.columns = ['投放次数', '总曝光', '平均曝光', '总访问', '平均访问', 
                            '总留资', '平均留资', '总转化金额', '平均转化金额', '总成本', '平均成本']
    
    # 按投放次数排序显示
    print(channel_stats.sort_values('投放次数', ascending=False))
    
    # 3. 关键指标统计
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("💰 核心指标统计")
    print("=" * 60)
    key_metrics = pd.DataFrame({
        '指标': ['曝光数', '访问数', '留资人数', '添加好友数', '转化人数', '转化金额', '投放成本'],
        '总量': [df['曝光数'].sum(), df['访问数'].sum(), df['留资人数'].sum(), 
                 df['添加好友数'].sum(), df['转化人数'].sum(), df['转化金额'].sum(), df['投放成本'].sum()],
        '均值': [df['曝光数'].mean(), df['访问数'].mean(), df['留资人数'].mean(),
                 df['添加好友数'].mean(), df['转化人数'].mean(), df['转化金额'].mean(), df['投放成本'].mean()],
        '最大值': [df['曝光数'].max(), df['访问数'].max(), df['留资人数'].max(),
                  df['添加好友数'].max(), df['转化人数'].max(), df['转化金额'].max(), df['投放成本'].max()]
    }).round(2)
    
    print(key_metrics)
    
    # 4. 销售人员分布
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("👥 销售人员分布")
    print("=" * 60)
    sales_stats = df.groupby('分配销售').agg({
        '转化金额': ['count', 'sum', 'mean'],
        '转化人数': ['sum', 'mean'],
        '添加好友数': ['sum', 'mean']
    }).round(2)
    
    sales_stats.columns = ['跟进次数', '总转化金额', '平均转化金额', '总转化人数', '平均转化人数', '总添加好友', '平均添加好友']
    print(sales_stats.sort_values('总转化金额', ascending=False))
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("✅ 任务1完成：数据基本特征探索")
    print("=" * 60)

    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 计算各渠道转化指标
    channel_performance = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '曝光数': 'sum',
        '访问数': 'sum',
        '留资人数': 'sum',
        '添加好友数': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum',
        '转化金额': 'sum',
        '投放成本': 'sum'
    }).round(2)
    
    # 计算关键转化率指标
    channel_performance['访问转化率'] = (channel_performance['访问数'] / channel_performance['曝光数'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_performance['留资转化率'] = (channel_performance['留资人数'] / channel_performance['访问数'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_performance['好友转化率'] = (channel_performance['添加好友数'] / channel_performance['留资人数'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_performance['最终转化率'] = (channel_performance['转化人数'] / channel_performance['访问数'] * 100).round(2)
    
    # 计算ROI
    channel_performance['ROI'] = ((channel_performance['转化金额'] - channel_performance['投放成本']) / channel_performance['投放成本'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_performance['每获客成本'] = (channel_performance['投放成本'] / channel_performance['转化人数']).round(2)
    channel_performance['客单价'] = (channel_performance['转化金额'] / channel_performance['转化人数']).round(2)
    
    # 处理除零错误
    channel_performance = channel_performance.replace([np.inf, -np.inf], 0)
    channel_performance = channel_performance.fillna(0)
    
    # 按ROI排序
    channel_performance_sorted = channel_performance.sort_values('ROI', ascending=False)
    
    print("📊 渠道综合效果排名（按ROI排序）：")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    display_columns = ['投放成本', '转化金额', 'ROI', '每获客成本', '客单价', '最终转化率', '访问转化率', '留资转化率']
    print(channel_performance_sorted[display_columns].round(2))
    
    # 识别明星渠道和问题渠道
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("🏆 渠道分类分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 明星渠道（ROI > 100%且转化人数 > 100）
    star_channels = channel_performance_sorted[
        (channel_performance_sorted['ROI'] > 100) & 
        (channel_performance_sorted['转化人数'] > 100)
    ]
    
    print("🌟 明星渠道（高ROI + 高转化量）：")
    if not star_channels.empty:
        for idx, row in star_channels.iterrows():
            print(f"   • {idx}: ROI {row['ROI']}%, 转化金额 ¥{row['转化金额']:,.0f}, 转化人数 {row['转化人数']:.0f}")
    else:
        print("   暂无明星渠道")
    
    # 潜力渠道（ROI高但量小）
    potential_channels = channel_performance_sorted[
        (channel_performance_sorted['ROI'] > 50) & 
        (channel_performance_sorted['转化人数'] <= 100)
    ]
    
    print("\n💎 潜力渠道（高ROI但规模小）：")
    if not potential_channels.empty:
        for idx, row in potential_channels.iterrows():
            print(f"   • {idx}: ROI {row['ROI']}%, 转化人数 {row['转化人数']:.0f}（建议加大投入）")
    else:
        print("   暂无潜力渠道")
    
    # 问题渠道（ROI为负或很低）
    problem_channels = channel_performance_sorted[channel_performance_sorted['ROI'] < 0]
    
    print("\n⚠️ 问题渠道（ROI为负）：")
    if not problem_channels.empty:
        for idx, row in problem_channels.iterrows():
            print(f"   • {idx}: ROI {row['ROI']}%, 投入 ¥{row['投放成本']:,.0f}, 损失 ¥{row['转化金额']-row['投放成本']:,.0f}")
    else:
        print("   暂无问题渠道")
    
    # 整体转化漏斗分析
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("🔄 整体转化漏斗分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    total_stats = df.agg({
        '曝光数': 'sum',
        '访问数': 'sum',
        '留资人数': 'sum',
        '添加好友数': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum'
    })
    
    print(f"曝光数 → 访问数: {total_stats['曝光数']:,} → {total_stats['访问数']:,} (转化率: {total_stats['访问数']/total_stats['曝光数']*100:.2f}%)")
    print(f"访问数 → 留资人数: {total_stats['访问数']:,} → {total_stats['留资人数']:,} (转化率: {total_stats['留资人数']/total_stats['访问数']*100:.2f}%)")
    print(f"留资人数 → 添加好友: {total_stats['留资人数']:,} → {total_stats['添加好友数']:,} (转化率: {total_stats['添加好友数']/total_stats['留资人数']*100:.2f}%)")
    print(f"访问数 → 转化人数: {total_stats['访问数']:,} → {total_stats['转化人数']:,} (最终转化率: {total_stats['转化人数']/total_stats['访问数']*100:.2f}%)")
    
    # 计算整体ROI
    total_revenue = df['转化金额'].sum()
    total_cost = df['投放成本'].sum()
    overall_roi = (total_revenue - total_cost) / total_cost * 100
    
    print(f"\n💰 整体ROI: ({total_revenue:,} - {total_cost:,}) / {total_cost:,} = {overall_roi:.2f}%")
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("✅ 任务2完成：渠道转化效果与ROI分析")
    print("=" * 60)

- 每个任务执行后标记为completed

- 即使报告已输出，也必须调用todo_write标记最后一个任务为completed

[2025-12-17 14:48:20] === 事件: tool_call ===
  工具: run_code
  任务ID: N/A
  代码:
    import pandas as pd
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    import numpy as np
    import os
    
    # 读取数据
    df = pd.read_excel(os.environ['DATASET_PATH'])
    
    print("=" * 60)
    print("👥 销售人员绩效评估")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 销售人员综合绩效分析
    sales_performance = df.groupby('分配销售').agg({
        '转化金额': ['sum', 'mean', 'count'],
        '转化人数': ['sum', 'mean'],
        '添加好友数': ['sum', 'mean'],
        '留资人数': 'sum',
        '投放成本': 'sum'
    }).round(2)
    
    sales_performance.columns = ['总转化金额', '平均转化金额', '跟进次数', 
                               '总转化人数', '平均转化人数',
                               '总添加好友', '平均添加好友', '总留资人数', '总投放成本']
    
    # 计算销售人员效率指标
    sales_performance['转化率'] = (sales_performance['总转化人数'] / sales_performance['总留资人数'] * 100).round(2)
    sales_performance['人效'] = (sales_performance['总转化金额'] / sales_performance['跟进次数']).round(2)
    sales_performance['客户价值'] = (sales_performance['总转化金额'] / sales_performance['总转化人数']).round(2)
    
    # 按总转化金额排序
    sales_performance_sorted = sales_performance.sort_values('总转化金额', ascending=False)
    
    print("📊 销售人员综合绩效排名：")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    display_cols = ['跟进次数', '总转化金额', '平均转化金额', '总转化人数', '转化率', '人效', '客户价值']
    print(sales_performance_sorted[display_cols])
    
    # 销售人员渠道分布分析
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📢 销售人员渠道分布与专长分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 每个销售人员在不同渠道的表现
    sales_channel_analysis = df.groupby(['分配销售', '投放渠道']).agg({
        '转化金额': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum',
        '投放成本': 'sum'
    }).round(2)
    
    # 计算每个销售的主要渠道（转化金额最高的渠道）
    for sales_person in sales_performance_sorted.index:
        person_data = df[df['分配销售'] == sales_person]
        channel_perf = person_data.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
            '转化金额': 'sum',
            '转化人数': 'sum'
        }).sort_values('转化金额', ascending=False)
        
        top_channel = channel_perf.index[0]
        top_channel_amount = channel_perf.iloc[0]['转化金额']
        top_channel_conversions = channel_perf.iloc[0]['转化人数']
        
        print(f"\n👤 {sales_person}:")
        print(f"   主渠道: {top_channel} (¥{top_channel_amount:,.0f}, {top_channel_conversions:.0f}人)")
        
        # 显示前3个渠道
        print("   渠道TOP3:")
        for i in range(min(3, len(channel_perf))):
            ch = channel_perf.index[i]
            amt = channel_perf.iloc[i]['转化金额']
            conv = channel_perf.iloc[i]['转化人数']
            print(f"      {i+1}. {ch}: ¥{amt:,.0f} ({conv:.0f}人)")
    
    # 销售人员效率对比
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("⚡ 销售人员效率对比")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 计算每个销售人员的平均处理时间（假设每次跟进花费相似时间）
    efficiency_metrics = pd.DataFrame({
        '销售人员': sales_performance_sorted.index,
        '人效(元/次)': sales_performance_sorted['人效'].values,
        '转化率(%)': sales_performance_sorted['转化率'].values,
        '客单价(元)': sales_performance_sorted['客户价值'].values,
        '平均转化人数': sales_performance_sorted['平均转化人数'].values
    })
    
    print(efficiency_metrics.round(2))
    
    # 识别最佳销售人员
    best_sales = sales_performance_sorted.index[0]
    best_sales_performance = sales_performance_sorted.iloc[0]
    
    print(f"\n🏆 最佳销售人员: {best_sales}")
    print(f"   • 总转化金额: ¥{best_sales_performance['总转化金额']:,.0f}")
    print(f"   • 总转化人数: {best_sales_performance['总转化人数']:.0f}人")
    print(f"   • 转化率: {best_sales_performance['转化率']:.2f}%")
    print(f"   • 人效: ¥{best_sales_performance['人效']:,.0f}/次")
    
    # 识别需要改进的销售人员
    print(f"\n📊 需要关注的人员:")
    for i in range(len(sales_performance_sorted)):
        if i > 0:  # 跳过第一名
            person = sales_performance_sorted.index[i]
            performance = sales_performance_sorted.iloc[i]
            
            # 与第一名对比
            gap = (best_sales_performance['总转化金额'] - performance['总转化金额']) / best_sales_performance['总转化金额'] * 100
            
            if gap > 50:  # 差距大于50%
                print(f"   • {person}: 转化金额差距 {gap:.1f}%，建议重点培训")
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("✅ 任务3完成：销售人员绩效评估")
    print("=" * 60)

[2025-12-17 14:49:01] === 事件: tool_call ===

  代码:
    import pandas as pd
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    import numpy as np
    import os
    
    # 读取数据
    df = pd.read_excel(os.environ['DATASET_PATH'])
    
    print("=" * 60)
    print("🔄 转化漏斗与流失率深度分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 整体转化漏斗计算
    total_funnel = {
        '曝光数': df['曝光数'].sum(),
        '访问数': df['访问数'].sum(),
        '留资人数': df['留资人数'].sum(),
        '添加好友数': df['添加好友数'].sum(),
        '转化人数': df['转化人数'].sum()
    }
    
    print("📊 整体转化漏斗：")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 计算各阶段转化率
    funnel_stages = ['曝光数', '访问数', '留资人数', '添加好友数', '转化人数']
    funnel_data = []
    
    for i in range(len(funnel_stages)):
        stage = funnel_stages[i]
        count = total_funnel[stage]
        
        if i == 0:
            conversion_rate = 100.0
            loss_amount = 0
            loss_rate = 0.0
        else:
            prev_stage = funnel_stages[i-1]
            prev_count = total_funnel[prev_stage]
            conversion_rate = count / prev_count * 100
            loss_amount = prev_count - count
            loss_rate = 100 - conversion_rate
        
        funnel_data.append({
            '阶段': stage,
            '数量': count,
            '转化率': conversion_rate,
            '流失量': loss_amount,
            '流失率': loss_rate
        })
        
        if i == 0:
            print(f"{stage}: {count:,} (基准)")
        else:
            print(f"{stage}: {count:,} (转化率: {conversion_rate:.2f}%, 流失: {loss_amount:,}, 流失率: {loss_rate:.2f}%)")
    
    # 创建漏斗DataFrame
    funnel_df = pd.DataFrame(funnel_data)
    funnel_df['阶段转化率'] = funnel_df['转化率'].diff()
    funnel_df.loc[0, '阶段转化率'] = 100.0
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📉 关键流失点分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 识别最大流失点
    max_loss_idx = funnel_df['流失率'].idxmax()
    max_loss_stage = funnel_df.loc[max_loss_idx, '阶段']
    max_loss_rate = funnel_df.loc[max_loss_idx, '流失率']
    
    print(f"⚠️ 最大流失点: {funnel_stages[max_loss_idx-1]} → {max_loss_stage}")
    print(f"   流失率: {max_loss_rate:.2f}%")
    print(f"   流失数量: {funnel_df.loc[max_loss_idx, '流失量']:,}")
    
    # 各渠道漏斗对比
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📊 各渠道转化漏斗对比")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 按渠道分析转化率
    channel_funnel = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '曝光数': 'sum',
        '访问数': 'sum',
        '留资人数': 'sum',
        '添加好友数': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum'
    })
    
    # 计算各渠道各阶段转化率
    channel_funnel['访问转化率'] = (channel_funnel['访问数'] / channel_funnel['曝光数'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_funnel['留资转化率'] = (channel_funnel['留资人数'] / channel_funnel['访问数'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_funnel['好友转化率'] = (channel_funnel['添加好友数'] / channel_funnel['留资人数'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_funnel['最终转化率'] = (channel_funnel['转化人数'] / channel_funnel['访问数'] * 100).round(2)
    
    # 找出各阶段表现最好和最差的渠道
    print("🎯 各阶段转化率最高/最低渠道：")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 访问转化率
    best_visit = channel_funnel['访问转化率'].idxmax()
    worst_visit = channel_funnel['访问转化率'].idxmin()
    print(f"访问转化率: 最高 {best_visit} ({channel_funnel.loc[best_visit, '访问转化率']:.2f}%)")
    print(f"            最低 {worst_visit} ({channel_funnel.loc[worst_visit, '访问转化率']:.2f}%)")
    
    # 留资转化率
    best_lead = channel_funnel['留资转化率'].idxmax()
    worst_lead = channel_funnel['留资转化率'].idxmin()
    print(f"留资转化率: 最高 {best_lead} ({channel_funnel.loc[best_lead, '留资转化率']:.2f}%)")
    print(f"            最低 {worst_lead} ({channel_funnel.loc[worst_lead, '留资转化率']:.2f}%)")
    
    # 最终转化率
    best_final = channel_funnel['最终转化率'].idxmax()
    worst_final = channel_funnel['最终转化率'].idxmin()
    print(f"最终转化率: 最高 {best_final} ({channel_funnel.loc[best_final, '最终转化率']:.2f}%)")
    print(f"            最低 {worst_final} ({channel_funnel.loc[worst_final, '最终转化率']:.2f}%)")
    
    # 销售人员漏斗分析
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("👥 销售人员转化效率分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    sales_funnel = df.groupby('分配销售').agg({
        '留资人数': 'sum',
        '添加好友数': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum'
    })
    
    sales_funnel['好友转化率'] = (sales_funnel['添加好友数'] / sales_funnel['留资人数'] * 100).round(2)
    sales_funnel['最终转化率'] = (sales_funnel['转化人数'] / sales_funnel['添加好友数'] * 100).round(2)
    sales_funnel['整体转化率'] = (sales_funnel['转化人数'] / sales_funnel['留资人数'] * 100).round(2)
    
    print("📈 销售人员转化能力对比：")
    print("-" * 60)
    print(sales_funnel[['好友转化率', '最终转化率', '整体转化率']].sort_values('整体转化率', ascending=False))
    
    # 流失率优化建议
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("💡 流失率优化建议")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    print("1. 曝光 → 访问阶段:")
    print(f"   • 当前转化率: {funnel_df.loc[1, '转化率']:.2f}%")
    print("   • 优化建议: 提升广告创意质量，优化投放定向")
    
    print(f"\n2. 访问 → 留资阶段:")
    print(f"   • 当前转化率: {funnel_df.loc[2, '转化率']:.2f}%")
    print("   • 优化建议: 优化落地页设计，简化留资流程，增加留资激励")
    
    print(f"\n3. 留资 → 添加好友阶段:")
    print(f"   • 当前转化率: {funnel_df.loc[3, '转化率']:.2f}%")
    print("   • 优化建议: 加强销售跟进及时性，优化首次沟通话术")
    
    print(f"\n4. 添加好友 → 最终转化阶段:")
    print(f"   • 当前转化率: {funnel_df.loc[4, '转化率']:.2f}%")
    print("   • 优化建议: 提升销售技巧，优化产品方案，增加客户信任")
    
    # 计算优化潜力
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📈 优化潜力分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    current_conversion = funnel_df.loc[4, '数量']
    total_visits = funnel_df.loc[1, '数量']
    
    # 如果每个环节提升10%
    target_improvement = 0.1
    optimized_visits = total_visits * (1 + target_improvement)
    optimized_leads = optimized_visits * (funnel_df.loc[2, '数量'] / funnel_df.loc[1, '数量']) * (1 + target_improvement)
    optimized_friends = optimized_leads * (funnel_df.loc[3, '数量'] / funnel_df.loc[2, '数量']) * (1 + target_improvement)
    optimized_conversions = optimized_friends * (funnel_df.loc[4, '数量'] / funnel_df.loc[3, '数量']) * (1 + target_improvement)
    
    potential_increase = optimized_conversions - current_conversion
    potential_revenue = potential_increase * (df['转化金额'].sum() / df['转化人数'].sum())
    
    print(f"当前转化人数: {current_conversion:,.0f}")
    print(f"如果各环节提升10%: {optimized_conversions:,.0f}")
    print(f"潜在增长: {potential_increase:,.0f} 人 ({potential_increase/current_conversion*100:.1f}%)")

  描述: 分析转化漏斗与流失率
  代码:
    import pandas as pd
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    import numpy as np
    import os
    
    # 读取数据
    df = pd.read_excel(os.environ['DATASET_PATH'])
    
    print("=" * 60)
    print("🔄 转化漏斗与流失率深度分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 整体转化漏斗计算
    total_funnel = {
        '曝光数': df['曝光数'].sum(),
        '访问数': df['访问数'].sum(),
        '留资人数': df['留资人数'].sum(),
        '添加好友数': df['添加好友数'].sum(),
        '转化人数': df['转化人数'].sum()
    }
    
    print("📊 整体转化漏斗：")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 计算各阶段转化率
    funnel_stages = ['曝光数', '访问数', '留资人数', '添加好友数', '转化人数']
    funnel_data = []
    
    for i in range(len(funnel_stages)):
        stage = funnel_stages[i]
        count = total_funnel[stage]
        
        if i == 0:
            conversion_rate = 100.0
            loss_amount = 0
            loss_rate = 0.0
        else:
            prev_stage = funnel_stages[i-1]
            prev_count = total_funnel[prev_stage]
            conversion_rate = count / prev_count * 100
            loss_amount = prev_count - count
            loss_rate = 100 - conversion_rate
        
        funnel_data.append({
            '阶段': stage,
            '数量': count,
            '转化率': conversion_rate,
            '流失量': loss_amount,
            '流失率': loss_rate
        })
        
        if i == 0:
            print(f"{stage}: {count:,} (基准)")
        else:
            print(f"{stage}: {count:,} (转化率: {conversion_rate:.2f}%, 流失: {loss_amount:,}, 流失率: {loss_rate:.2f}%)")
    
    # 创建漏斗DataFrame
    funnel_df = pd.DataFrame(funnel_data)
    funnel_df['阶段转化率'] = funnel_df['转化率'].diff()
    funnel_df.loc[0, '阶段转化率'] = 100.0
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📉 关键流失点分析")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 识别最大流失点
    max_loss_idx = funnel_df['流失率'].idxmax()
    max_loss_stage = funnel_df.loc[max_loss_idx, '阶段']
    max_loss_rate = funnel_df.loc[max_loss_idx, '流失率']
    
    print(f"⚠️ 最大流失点: {funnel_stages[max_loss_idx-1]} → {max_loss_stage}")
    print(f"   流失率: {max_loss_rate:.2f}%")
    print(f"   流失数量: {funnel_df.loc[max_loss_idx, '流失量']:,}")
    
    # 各渠道漏斗对比
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📊 各渠道转化漏斗对比")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 按渠道分析转化率
    channel_funnel = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '曝光数': 'sum',
        '访问数': 'sum',
        '留资人数': 'sum',
        '添加好友数': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum'
    })
    
    # 计算各渠道各阶段转化率
    channel_funnel['访问转化率'] = (channel_funnel['访问数'] / channel_funnel['曝光数'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_funnel['留资转化率'] = (channel_funnel['留资人数'] / channel_funnel['访问数'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_funnel['好友转化率'] = (channel_funnel['添加好友数'] / channel_funnel['留资人数'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_funnel['最终转化率'] = (channel_funnel['转化人数'] / channel_funnel['访问数'] * 100).round(2)
    
    # 找出各阶段表现最好和最差的渠道
    print("🎯 各阶段转化率最高/最低渠道：")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 访问转化率
    best_visit = channel_funnel['访问转化率'].idxmax()
    worst_visit = channel_funnel['访问转化率'].idxmin()
    print(f"访问转化率: 最高 {best_visit} ({channel_funnel.loc[best_visit, '访问转化率']:.2f}%)")
    print(f"            最低 {worst_visit} ({channel_funnel.loc[worst_visit, '访问转化率']:.2f}%)")
    
    # 留资转化率
    best_lead = channel_funnel['留资转化率'].idxmax()
    worst_lead = channel_funnel['留资转化率'].idxmin()
    print(f"留资转化率: 最高 {best_lead} ({channel_funnel.loc[best_lead, '留资转化率']:.2f}%)")
    print(f"            最低 {worst_lead} ({channel_funnel.loc[worst_lead, '留资转化率']:.2f}%)")
    
    # 最终转化率
    best_final = channel_funnel['最终转化率'].idxmax()
    worst_final = channel_funnel['最终转化率'].idxmin()
    print(f"最终转化率: 最高 {best_final} ({channel_funnel.loc[best_final, '最终转化率']:.2f}%)")
    print(f"            最低 {worst_final} ({channel_funnel.loc[worst_final, '最终转化率']:.2f}%)")
    
    # 销售人员漏斗分析
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)

        '留资人数': 'sum',

[2025-12-17 14:49:47] === 事件: tool_call ===
  工具: run_code
  任务ID: N/A
  代码:
    import pandas as pd
    import numpy as np
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    from sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression
    from sklearn.preprocessing import PolynomialFeatures
    import os
    
    # 读取数据
    df = pd.read_excel(os.environ['DATASET_PATH'])
    
    print("=" * 60)
    print("📈 建立预测模型并制定未来规划")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 1. 渠道投资优化建议
    print("💰 渠道投资优化建议")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 计算各渠道ROI和转化效率
    channel_roi = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '投放成本': 'sum',
        '转化金额': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum',
        '访问数': 'sum'
    }).round(2)
    
    channel_roi['ROI'] = ((channel_roi['转化金额'] - channel_roi['投放成本']) / channel_roi['投放成本'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_roi['每获客成本'] = (channel_roi['投放成本'] / channel_roi['转化人数']).round(2)
    channel_roi['客单价'] = (channel_roi['转化金额'] / channel_roi['转化人数']).round(2)
    channel_roi['转化率'] = (channel_roi['转化人数'] / channel_roi['访问数'] * 100).round(4)
    
    # 渠道分级
    star_channels = channel_roi[(channel_roi['ROI'] > 100) & (channel_roi['转化人数'] > 1000)]
    growth_channels = channel_roi[(channel_roi['ROI'] > 50) & (channel_roi['ROI'] <= 100)]
    problem_channels = channel_roi[channel_roi['ROI'] < 0]
    
    print("🌟 明星渠道（加大投入）:")
    for idx, row in star_channels.iterrows():
        recommended_investment = row['投放成本'] * 1.5  # 建议增加50%投入
        expected_return = recommended_investment * (1 + row['ROI'] / 100)
        print(f"   • {idx}: 当前投入 ¥{row['投放成本']:,.0f}, 建议增至 ¥{recommended_investment:,.0f}")
        print(f"     预期回报: ¥{expected_return:,.0f} (ROI: {row['ROI']:.1f}%)")
    
    print("\n💎 增长渠道（适度投入）:")
    for idx, row in growth_channels.iterrows():
        print(f"   • {idx}: ROI {row['ROI']:.1f}%, 建议维持或小幅增加投入")
    
    print("\n⚠️ 问题渠道（优化或暂停）:")
    for idx, row in problem_channels.iterrows():
        loss = row['转化金额'] - row['投放成本']
        print(f"   • {idx}: 当前亏损 ¥{loss:,.0f}, 建议: 优化策略或暂停投放")
    
    # 2. 销售团队优化建议
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("👥 销售团队优化建议")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 分析销售人员效率
    sales_performance = df.groupby('分配销售').agg({
        '转化金额': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum',
        '添加好友数': 'sum',
        '留资人数': 'sum'
    })
    
    sales_performance['转化率'] = (sales_performance['转化人数'] / sales_performance['添加好友数'] * 100).round(2)
    sales_performance['好友转化率'] = (sales_performance['添加好友数'] / sales_performance['留资人数'] * 100).round(2)
    sales_performance['人效'] = (sales_performance['转化金额'] / len(df[df['分配销售'] == sales_performance.index[0]])).round(2)
    
    print("🏆 优秀销售人员标杆:")
    best_sales = sales_performance.loc[sales_performance['转化率'].idxmax()]
    print(f"   • {sales_performance['转化率'].idxmax()}: 转化率 {best_sales['转化率']:.2f}%")
    print(f"   • 经验总结: 快速响应、精准跟进、专业能力强")
    
    print("\n📚 培训提升计划:")
    for sales_name, row in sales_performance.iterrows():
        if row['转化率'] < best_sales['转化率'] * 0.8:  # 低于最佳销售80%
            gap = best_sales['转化率'] - row['转化率']
            print(f"   • {sales_name}: 转化率差距 {gap:.2f}个百分点")
            print(f"     建议: 话术培训、案例学习、导师带教")
    
    # 3. 转化漏斗优化目标
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("🎯 转化漏斗优化目标")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 当前漏斗数据
    current_funnel = {
        '访问转化率': 16.13,  # 曝光→访问
        '留资转化率': 35.30,  # 访问→留资
        '好友转化率': 6.92,   # 留资→好友
        '最终转化率': 33.94   # 好友→转化
    }
    
    # 设定优化目标（每个环节提升20%）
    target_improvement = 0.2
    target_funnel = {k: v * (1 + target_improvement) for k, v in current_funnel.items()}
    
    print("📊 转化漏斗优化目标（提升20%）:")
    for stage, current_rate in current_funnel.items():
        target_rate = target_funnel[stage]
        print(f"   • {stage}: {current_rate:.2f}% → {target_rate:.2f}%")
    
    # 计算优化后的效果
    current_monthly_visits = df['访问数'].sum()
    current_monthly_conversions = df['转化人数'].sum()
    
    optimized_visits = current_monthly_visits * (target_funnel['访问转化率'] / current_funnel['访问转化率'])
    optimized_leads = optimized_visits * (target_funnel['留资转化率'] / 100)
    optimized_friends = optimized_leads * (target_funnel['好友转化率'] / 100)
    optimized_conversions = optimized_friends * (target_funnel['最终转化率'] / 100)
    
    growth_rate = (optimized_conversions - current_monthly_conversions) / current_monthly_conversions * 100
    
    print(f"\n💰 优化效果预测:")
    print(f"   • 当前月转化: {current_monthly_conversions:,.0f} 人")
    print(f"   • 优化后月转化: {optimized_conversions:,.0f} 人")
    print(f"   • 增长潜力: {optimized_conversions - current_monthly_conversions:,.0f} 人 (+{growth_rate:.1f}%)")
    print(f"   • 预期增收: ¥{(optimized_conversions - current_monthly_conversions) * df['转化金额'].sum() / df['转化人数'].sum():,.0f}")
    
    # 4. 未来6个月增长规划
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📅 未来6个月增长规划")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 基于历史数据建立简单预测模型
    # 假设每月投放成本增加10%，ROI保持稳定
    monthly_cost = df['投放成本'].sum()
    monthly_revenue = df['转化金额'].sum()
    monthly_roi = monthly_revenue / monthly_cost
    
    current_month = 1
    projections = []
    
    for month in range(1, 7):
        # 每月成本增长10%
        projected_cost = monthly_cost * (1.1 ** (month - 1))
        
        # 考虑漏斗优化效果（每月优化5%）
        optimization_factor = 1 + (month * 0.05)
        
        # 计算预期收入
        projected_revenue = projected_cost * monthly_roi * optimization_factor
        projected_profit = projected_revenue - projected_cost
        
        projections.append({
            '月份': f'第{month}月',
            '投放成本': projected_cost,
            '预期收入': projected_revenue,
            '预期利润': projected_profit,
            'ROI': (projected_profit / projected_cost * 100)
        })
        
        print(f"{projections[-1]['月份']}:")
        print(f"   投放成本: ¥{projected_cost:,.0f}")
        print(f"   预期收入: ¥{projected_revenue:,.0f}")
        print(f"   预期利润: ¥{projected_profit:,.0f}")
        print(f"   ROI: {projections[-1]['ROI']:.1f}%")
        print()
    
    # 5. 具体行动计划
    print("=" * 60)
    print("🚀 具体行动计划")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    print("📋 短期行动（1-2个月）:")
    print("   1. 渠道优化:")
    print("      • 增加SEO-B关键词投入50%（当前ROI最高）")
    print("      • 暂停社媒-A/B/C达人投放（ROI为负）")
    print("      • 优化SEM-A关键词策略或暂停")
    print("   2. 销售培训:")
    print("      • 组织王XX分享成功经验")
    print("      • 针对赵XX进行一对一辅导")
    print("   3. 漏斗优化:")
    print("      • 简化留资流程，目标提升留资转化率至40%")
    print("      • 建立销售跟进SOP，24小时内必须添加好友")

    print("   1. 渠道拓展:")

    import pandas as pd
    import numpy as np
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    from sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression
    from sklearn.preprocessing import PolynomialFeatures
    import os
    
    # 读取数据
    df = pd.read_excel(os.environ['DATASET_PATH'])
    
    print("=" * 60)
    print("📈 建立预测模型并制定未来规划")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 1. 渠道投资优化建议
    print("💰 渠道投资优化建议")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 计算各渠道ROI和转化效率
    channel_roi = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '投放成本': 'sum',
        '转化金额': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum',
        '访问数': 'sum'
    }).round(2)
    
    channel_roi['ROI'] = ((channel_roi['转化金额'] - channel_roi['投放成本']) / channel_roi['投放成本'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_roi['每获客成本'] = (channel_roi['投放成本'] / channel_roi['转化人数']).round(2)
    channel_roi['客单价'] = (channel_roi['转化金额'] / channel_roi['转化人数']).round(2)
    channel_roi['转化率'] = (channel_roi['转化人数'] / channel_roi['访问数'] * 100).round(4)
    
    # 渠道分级
    star_channels = channel_roi[(channel_roi['ROI'] > 100) & (channel_roi['转化人数'] > 1000)]
    growth_channels = channel_roi[(channel_roi['ROI'] > 50) & (channel_roi['ROI'] <= 100)]
    problem_channels = channel_roi[channel_roi['ROI'] < 0]
    
    print("🌟 明星渠道（加大投入）:")
    for idx, row in star_channels.iterrows():
        recommended_investment = row['投放成本'] * 1.5  # 建议增加50%投入
        expected_return = recommended_investment * (1 + row['ROI'] / 100)
        print(f"   • {idx}: 当前投入 ¥{row['投放成本']:,.0f}, 建议增至 ¥{recommended_investment:,.0f}")
        print(f"     预期回报: ¥{expected_return:,.0f} (ROI: {row['ROI']:.1f}%)")
    
    print("\n💎 增长渠道（适度投入）:")
    for idx, row in growth_channels.iterrows():
        print(f"   • {idx}: ROI {row['ROI']:.1f}%, 建议维持或小幅增加投入")
    
    print("\n⚠️ 问题渠道（优化或暂停）:")
    for idx, row in problem_channels.iterrows():
        loss = row['转化金额'] - row['投放成本']
        print(f"   • {idx}: 当前亏损 ¥{loss:,.0f}, 建议: 优化策略或暂停投放")
    
    # 2. 销售团队优化建议
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("👥 销售团队优化建议")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 分析销售人员效率
    sales_performance = df.groupby('分配销售').agg({
        '转化金额': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum',
        '添加好友数': 'sum',
        '留资人数': 'sum'
    })
    
    sales_performance['转化率'] = (sales_performance['转化人数'] / sales_performance['添加好友数'] * 100).round(2)
    sales_performance['好友转化率'] = (sales_performance['添加好友数'] / sales_performance['留资人数'] * 100).round(2)
    sales_performance['人效'] = (sales_performance['转化金额'] / len(df[df['分配销售'] == sales_performance.index[0]])).round(2)
    
    print("🏆 优秀销售人员标杆:")
    best_sales = sales_performance.loc[sales_performance['转化率'].idxmax()]
    print(f"   • {sales_performance['转化率'].idxmax()}: 转化率 {best_sales['转化率']:.2f}%")
    print(f"   • 经验总结: 快速响应、精准跟进、专业能力强")
    
    print("\n📚 培训提升计划:")
    for sales_name, row in sales_performance.iterrows():
        if row['转化率'] < best_sales['转化率'] * 0.8:  # 低于最佳销售80%
            gap = best_sales['转化率'] - row['转化率']
            print(f"   • {sales_name}: 转化率差距 {gap:.2f}个百分点")
            print(f"     建议: 话术培训、案例学习、导师带教")
    
    # 3. 转化漏斗优化目标
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("🎯 转化漏斗优化目标")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 当前漏斗数据
    current_funnel = {
        '访问转化率': 16.13,  # 曝光→访问
        '留资转化率': 35.30,  # 访问→留资
        '好友转化率': 6.92,   # 留资→好友
        '最终转化率': 33.94   # 好友→转化
    }
    
    # 设定优化目标（每个环节提升20%）
    target_improvement = 0.2
    target_funnel = {k: v * (1 + target_improvement) for k, v in current_funnel.items()}
    
    print("📊 转化漏斗优化目标（提升20%）:")
    for stage, current_rate in current_funnel.items():
        target_rate = target_funnel[stage]
        print(f"   • {stage}: {current_rate:.2f}% → {target_rate:.2f}%")
    
    # 计算优化后的效果
    current_monthly_visits = df['访问数'].sum()
    current_monthly_conversions = df['转化人数'].sum()
    
    optimized_visits = current_monthly_visits * (target_funnel['访问转化率'] / current_funnel['访问转化率'])
    optimized_leads = optimized_visits * (target_funnel['留资转化率'] / 100)
    optimized_friends = optimized_leads * (target_funnel['好友转化率'] / 100)
    optimized_conversions = optimized_friends * (target_funnel['最终转化率'] / 100)
    
    growth_rate = (optimized_conversions - current_monthly_conversions) / current_monthly_conversions * 100
    
    print(f"\n💰 优化效果预测:")
    print(f"   • 当前月转化: {current_monthly_conversions:,.0f} 人")
    print(f"   • 优化后月转化: {optimized_conversions:,.0f} 人")
    print(f"   • 增长潜力: {optimized_conversions - current_monthly_conversions:,.0f} 人 (+{growth_rate:.1f}%)")
    print(f"   • 预期增收: ¥{(optimized_conversions - current_monthly_conversions) * df['转化金额'].sum() / df['转化人数'].sum():,.0f}")
    
    # 4. 未来6个月增长规划
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📅 未来6个月增长规划")
    print("-" * 60)

    sales_performance['好友转化率'] = (sales_performance['添加好友数'] / sales_performance['留资人数'] * 100).round(2)
    sales_performance['人效'] = (sales_performance['转化金额'] / len(df[df['分配销售'] == sales_performance.index[0]])).round(2)
    
    print("🏆 优秀销售人员标杆:")
    best_sales_name = sales_performance['转化率'].idxmax()
    best_sales = sales_performance.loc[best_sales_name]
    print(f"   • {best_sales_name}: 转化率 {best_sales['转化率']:.2f}%")
    print(f"   • 经验总结: 快速响应、精准跟进、专业能力强")
    
    print("\n📚 培训提升计划:")
    for sales_name, row in sales_performance.iterrows():
        if row['转化率'] < best_sales['转化率'] * 0.8:  # 低于最佳销售80%
            gap = best_sales['转化率'] - row['转化率']
            print(f"   • {sales_name}: 转化率差距 {gap:.2f}个百分点")
            print(f"     建议: 话术培训、案例学习、导师带教")
    
    # 3. 转化漏斗优化目标
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("🎯 转化漏斗优化目标")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 当前漏斗数据
    current_funnel = {
        '访问转化率': 16.13,  # 曝光→访问
        '留资转化率': 35.30,  # 访问→留资
        '好友转化率': 6.92,   # 留资→好友
        '最终转化率': 33.94   # 好友→转化
    }
    
    # 设定优化目标（每个环节提升20%）
    target_improvement = 0.2
    target_funnel = {k: v * (1 + target_improvement) for k, v in current_funnel.items()}
    
    print("📊 转化漏斗优化目标（提升20%）:")
    for stage, current_rate in current_funnel.items():
        target_rate = target_funnel[stage]
        print(f"   • {stage}: {current_rate:.2f}% → {target_rate:.2f}%")
    
    # 计算优化后的效果
    current_monthly_visits = df['访问数'].sum()
    current_monthly_conversions = df['转化人数'].sum()
    
    optimized_visits = current_monthly_visits * (target_funnel['访问转化率'] / current_funnel['访问转化率'])
    optimized_leads = optimized_visits * (target_funnel['留资转化率'] / 100)
    optimized_friends = optimized_leads * (target_funnel['好友转化率'] / 100)
    optimized_conversions = optimized_friends * (target_funnel['最终转化率'] / 100)
    
    growth_rate = (optimized_conversions - current_monthly_conversions) / current_monthly_conversions * 100
    avg_order_value = df['转化金额'].sum() / df['转化人数'].sum()
    
    print(f"\n💰 优化效果预测:")
    print(f"   • 当前月转化: {current_monthly_conversions:,.0f} 人")
    print(f"   • 优化后月转化: {optimized_conversions:,.0f} 人")
    print(f"   • 增长潜力: {optimized_conversions - current_monthly_conversions:,.0f} 人 (+{growth_rate:.1f}%)")
    print(f"   • 预期增收: ¥{(optimized_conversions - current_monthly_conversions) * avg_order_value:,.0f}")
    
    # 4. 未来6个月增长规划
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("📅 未来6个月增长规划")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 基于历史数据建立简单预测模型
    monthly_cost = df['投放成本'].sum()
    monthly_revenue = df['转化金额'].sum()
    monthly_roi = monthly_revenue / monthly_cost
    
    print("月度增长预测（成本+10%/月，优化+5%/月）:")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    for month in range(1, 7):
        # 每月成本增长10%
        projected_cost = monthly_cost * (1.1 ** (month - 1))
        
        # 考虑漏斗优化效果（每月优化5%）
        optimization_factor = 1 + (month * 0.05)
        
        # 计算预期收入
        projected_revenue = projected_cost * monthly_roi * optimization_factor
        projected_profit = projected_revenue - projected_cost
        
        print(f"第{month}月:")
        print(f"   投放成本: ¥{projected_cost:,.0f}")
        print(f"   预期收入: ¥{projected_revenue:,.0f}")
        print(f"   预期利润: ¥{projected_profit:,.0f}")
        print(f"   ROI: {projected_profit / projected_cost * 100:.1f}%")
        print()
    
    # 5. 具体行动计划
    print("=" * 60)

    import pandas as pd
    import numpy as np
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    import os
    
    # 读取数据
    df = pd.read_excel(os.environ['DATASET_PATH'])
    
    print("=" * 60)
    print("📈 建立预测模型并制定未来规划")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # 1. 渠道投资优化建议
    print("💰 渠道投资优化建议")
    print("-" * 60)
    
    # 计算各渠道ROI和转化效率
    channel_roi = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '投放成本': 'sum',
        '转化金额': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum',
        '访问数': 'sum'
    }).round(2)
    
    channel_roi['ROI'] = ((channel_roi['转化金额'] - channel_roi['投放成本']) / channel_roi['投放成本'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_roi['每获客成本'] = (channel_roi['投放成本'] / channel_roi['转化人数']).round(2)
    channel_roi['客单价'] = (channel_roi['转化金额'] / channel_roi['转化人数']).round(2)
    channel_roi['转化率'] = (channel_roi['转化人数'] / channel_roi['访问数'] * 100).round(4)
    
    # 渠道分级
    star_channels = channel_roi[(channel_roi['ROI'] > 100) & (channel_roi['转化人数'] > 1000)]
    growth_channels = channel_roi[(channel_roi['ROI'] > 50) & (channel_roi['ROI'] <= 100)]
    problem_channels = channel_roi[channel_roi['ROI'] < 0]
    
    print("🌟 明星渠道（加大投入）:")
    for idx, row in star_channels.iterrows():
        recommended_investment = row['投放成本'] * 1.5  # 建议增加50%投入
        expected_return = recommended_investment * (1 + row['ROI'] / 100)
        print(f"   • {idx}: 当前投入 ¥{row['投放成本']:,.0f}, 建议增至 ¥{recommended_investment:,.0f}")
        print(f"     预期回报: ¥{expected_return:,.0f} (ROI: {row['ROI']:.1f}%)")
    
    print("\n💎 增长渠道（适度投入）:")
    for idx, row in growth_channels.iterrows():
        print(f"   • {idx}: ROI {row['ROI']:.1f}%, 建议维持或小幅增加投入")
    
    print("\n⚠️ 问题渠道（优化或暂停）:")
    for idx, row in problem_channels.iterrows():
        loss = row['转化金额'] - row['投放成本']
        print(f"   • {idx}: 当前亏损 ¥{loss:,.0f}, 建议: 优化策略或暂停投放")
    
    # 2. 销售团队优化建议
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("👥 销售团队优化建议")
    print("-" * 60)

        '转化金额': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum',
        '添加好友数': 'sum',

    })

    sales_performance['好友转化率'] = (sales_performance['添加好友数'] / sales_performance['留资人数'] * 100).round(2)

    print(f"\n👥 团队目标:")
    print(f"   • 销售团队: 6人 → 10人")
    print(f"   • 人均产能: 提升30%")
    print(f"   • 转化率: 提升20%")
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("✅ 任务5完成：预测模型与未来规划")
    print("=" * 60)

  代码:
    import pandas as pd
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    import numpy as np
    import os
    
    # 读取数据
    df = pd.read_excel(os.environ['DATASET_PATH'])
    
    # 设置中文字体
    plt.rcParams['font.sans-serif'] = ['Arial Unicode MS', 'SimHei']
    plt.rcParams['axes.unicode_minus'] = False
    
    # 创建大图
    fig = plt.figure(figsize=(20, 16))
    
    # 1. 渠道ROI对比图
    ax1 = plt.subplot(2, 3, 1)
    channel_roi = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '投放成本': 'sum',
        '转化金额': 'sum'
    })
    channel_roi['ROI'] = ((channel_roi['转化金额'] - channel_roi['投放成本']) / channel_roi['投放成本'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_roi_sorted = channel_roi.sort_values('ROI', ascending=True)
    
    colors = ['red' if x < 0 else 'green' if x > 100 else 'orange' for x in channel_roi_sorted['ROI']]
    bars = ax1.barh(range(len(channel_roi_sorted)), channel_roi_sorted['ROI'], color=colors, alpha=0.7)
    ax1.set_yticks(range(len(channel_roi_sorted)))
    ax1.set_yticklabels(channel_roi_sorted.index, fontsize=10)
    ax1.set_xlabel('ROI (%)', fontsize=11)
    ax1.set_title('各渠道ROI对比', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')
    ax1.axvline(x=0, color='black', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5)
    
    # 添加数值标签
    for i, bar in enumerate(bars):
        width = bar.get_width()
        ax1.text(width + (20 if width >= 0 else -20), bar.get_y() + bar.get_height()/2, 
                 f'{width:.1f}%', ha='left' if width >= 0 else 'right', va='center', fontsize=9)
    
    # 2. 转化漏斗图
    ax2 = plt.subplot(2, 3, 2)
    funnel_data = [15519019, 2503749, 883836, 61182, 20763]
    funnel_labels = ['曝光数', '访问数', '留资人数', '添加好友数', '转化人数']
    funnel_colors = ['#FF9999', '#FFCC99', '#FFFF99', '#CCFF99', '#99FF99']
    
    bars = ax2.bar(funnel_labels, funnel_data, color=funnel_colors, alpha=0.7)
    ax2.set_title('转化漏斗分析', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')
    ax2.set_ylabel('数量', fontsize=11)
    ax2.tick_params(axis='x', rotation=45)
    
    # 添加数值标签
    for bar in bars:
        height = bar.get_height()
        ax2.text(bar.get_x() + bar.get_width()/2., height + height*0.01,
                 f'{int(height):,}', ha='center', va='bottom', fontsize=9, rotation=45)
    
    # 3. 销售人员绩效对比
    ax3 = plt.subplot(2, 3, 3)
    sales_performance = df.groupby('分配销售').agg({
        '转化金额': 'sum',
        '转化人数': 'sum'
    })
    sales_performance_sorted = sales_performance.sort_values('转化金额', ascending=False)
    
    bars = ax3.bar(sales_performance_sorted.index, sales_performance_sorted['转化金额']/10000, 
                   color=['gold' if i == 0 else 'silver' if i == 1 else '#CD7F32' if i == 2 else 'lightblue' 
                          for i in range(len(sales_performance_sorted))], alpha=0.8)
    ax3.set_title('销售人员转化金额对比', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')
    ax3.set_ylabel('转化金额 (万元)', fontsize=11)
    ax3.tick_params(axis='x', rotation=0)
    
    # 添加数值标签
    for bar in bars:
        height = bar.get_height()
        ax3.text(bar.get_x() + bar.get_width()/2., height + height*0.01,
                 f'{height:.1f}', ha='center', va='bottom', fontsize=10)
    
    # 4. 渠道转化人数对比
    ax4 = plt.subplot(2, 3, 4)
    channel_conversions = df.groupby('投放渠道')['转化人数'].sum().sort_values(ascending=True)
    
    bars = ax4.barh(range(len(channel_conversions)), channel_conversions.values, 
                    color=plt.cm.viridis(np.linspace(0, 1, len(channel_conversions))), alpha=0.7)
    ax4.set_yticks(range(len(channel_conversions)))
    ax4.set_yticklabels(channel_conversions.index, fontsize=10)
    ax4.set_xlabel('转化人数', fontsize=11)
    ax4.set_title('各渠道转化人数对比', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')
    
    # 添加数值标签
    for i, bar in enumerate(bars):
        width = bar.get_width()
        ax4.text(width + width*0.01, bar.get_y() + bar.get_height()/2,
                 f'{int(width)}', ha='left', va='center', fontsize=9)
    
    # 5. 未来6个月增长预测
    ax5 = plt.subplot(2, 3, 5)
    months = ['第1月', '第2月', '第3月', '第4月', '第5月', '第6月']
    monthly_cost = df['投放成本'].sum()
    monthly_revenue = df['转化金额'].sum()
    monthly_roi = monthly_revenue / monthly_cost
    
    projected_revenues = []
    projected_profits = []
    
    for month in range(1, 7):
        projected_cost = monthly_cost * (1.1 ** (month - 1))
        optimization_factor = 1 + (month * 0.05)
        projected_revenue = projected_cost * monthly_roi * optimization_factor
        projected_profit = projected_revenue - projected_cost
        
        projected_revenues.append(projected_revenue/10000)
        projected_profits.append(projected_profit/10000)
    
    ax5.plot(months, projected_revenues, marker='o', linewidth=2, label='预期收入', color='green')
    ax5.plot(months, projected_profits, marker='s', linewidth=2, label='预期利润', color='blue')
    ax5.set_title('未来6个月增长预测', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')
    ax5.set_ylabel('金额 (万元)', fontsize=11)
    ax5.legend()
    ax5.tick_params(axis='x', rotation=45)
    ax5.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
    
    # 6. 投放成本vs转化金额散点图
    ax6 = plt.subplot(2, 3, 6)
    channel_scatter = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '投放成本': 'sum',
        '转化金额': 'sum'
    }).round(2)
    
    scatter = ax6.scatter(channel_scatter['投放成本']/10000, channel_scatter['转化金额']/10000, 
                         s=100, alpha=0.7, c=range(len(channel_scatter)), cmap='viridis')
    ax6.set_xlabel('投放成本 (万元)', fontsize=11)
    ax6.set_ylabel('转化金额 (万元)', fontsize=11)
    ax6.set_title('渠道投入产出分析', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')
    
    # 添加45度参考线（ROI=100%）
    max_val = max(channel_scatter['投放成本'].max(), channel_scatter['转化金额'].max()) / 10000
    ax6.plot([0, max_val], [0, max_val], 'r--', alpha=0.5, label='ROI=100%')
    ax6.legend()
    
    # 添加渠道标签
    for idx, (channel, row) in enumerate(channel_scatter.iterrows()):
        ax6.annotate(channel, (row['投放成本']/10000, row['转化金额']/10000), 
                    xytext=(5, 5), textcoords='offset points', fontsize=8, alpha=0.8)
    
    plt.tight_layout()
    plt.savefig('result.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')
    plt.close()
    
    print("=" * 60)
    print("✅ 任务6完成：可视化图表已生成")

    import pandas as pd
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    import numpy as np
    import os
    
    # 读取数据
    df = pd.read_excel(os.environ['DATASET_PATH'])
    
    # 设置中文字体
    plt.rcParams['font.sans-serif'] = ['Arial Unicode MS', 'SimHei']
    plt.rcParams['axes.unicode_minus'] = False
    
    # 创建大图
    fig = plt.figure(figsize=(20, 16))
    
    # 1. 渠道ROI对比图
    ax1 = plt.subplot(2, 3, 1)
    channel_roi = df.groupby('投放渠道').agg({
        '投放成本': 'sum',
        '转化金额': 'sum'
    })
    channel_roi['ROI'] = ((channel_roi['转化金额'] - channel_roi['投放成本']) / channel_roi['投放成本'] * 100).round(2)
    channel_roi_sorted = channel_roi.sort_values('ROI', ascending=True)
    
    colors = ['red' if x < 0 else 'green' if x > 100 else 'orange' for x in channel_roi_sorted['ROI']]
    bars = ax1.barh(range(len(channel_roi_sorted)), channel_roi_sorted['ROI'], color=colors, alpha=0.7)
    ax1.set_yticks(range(len(channel_roi_sorted)))
    ax1.set_yticklabels(channel_roi_sorted.index, fontsize=10)
    ax1.set_xlabel('ROI (%)', fontsize=11)
    ax1.set_title('各渠道ROI对比', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')
    ax1.axvline(x=0, color='black', linestyle='--', alpha=0.5)
    
    # 添加数值标签
    for i, bar in enumerate(bars):
        width = bar.get_width()
        ax1.text(width + (20 if width >= 0 else -20), bar.get_y() + bar.get_height()/2, 
                 f'{width:.1f}%', ha='left' if width >= 0 else 'right', va='center', fontsize=9)
    
    # 2. 转化漏斗图
    ax2 = plt.subplot(2, 3, 2)
    funnel_data = [15519019, 2503749, 883836, 61182, 20763]
    funnel_labels = ['曝光数', '访问数', '留资人数', '添加好友数', '转化人数']
    funnel_colors = ['#FF9999', '#FFCC99', '#FFFF99', '#CCFF99', '#99FF99']
    
    bars = ax2.bar(funnel_labels, funnel_data, color=funnel_colors, alpha=0.7)
    ax2.set_title('转化漏斗分析', fontsize=12, fontweight='bold')
    ax2.set_ylabel('数量', fontsize=11)
    ax2.tick_params(axis='x', rotation=45)

                 f'{int(height):,}', ha='center', va='bottom', fontsize=9, rotation=45)
